[30;1m181 | [0m[35m  both `START` and `END` are color value strings.[0m
[30;1m182 | [0m[35m- ``'hald:'``, creates a Higher And Lower Dimension matrix table.[0m

[30;1m184 | [0m[35m- ``'label:TEXT'``, where `TEXT` is a string message.[0m
